V\u1edbi nh\u1eefng ki\u1ebfn tr\u00fac n\u00e0y, c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 Scroll s\u1ebd thu h\u00fat ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng h\u01a1n nh\u1edd s\u1ef1 v\u1eefng ch\u1eafc c\u1ee7a m\u1ea1ng v\u00e0 s\u1ef1 b\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 kh\u1ecfi nh\u1eefng MEV \n\n\u0110i\u1ec3m y\u1ebfu:\n\n- Scroll ch\u01b0a c\u00f3 token ri\u00eang c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh, do \u0111\u00f3 n\u00f3 ch\u01b0a c\u00f3 m\u1ed9t c\u01a1 ch\u1ebf kinh t\u1ebf r\u00f5 r\u00e0ng \u0111\u1ec3 khuy\u1ebfn kh\u00edch v\u00e0 \u0111i\u1ec1u ph\u1ed1i h\u00e0nh vi c\u1ee7a c\u00e1c b\u00ean li\u00ean quan trong h\u1ec7 sinh th\u00e1 \u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 l\u00e0m gi\u1ea3m s\u1ef1 tham gia c\u1ee7a c\u1ed9ng \u0111\u1ed3ng.\n- Scroll c\u00f2n m\u1edbi m\u1ebb v\u00e0 ch\u01b0a \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c ki\u1ec3m tra k\u1ef9 l\u01b0\u1ee1ng v\u1ec1 t\u00ednh an to\u00e0n v\u00e0 \u1ed5n \u0111\u1ecbnh. Many investors utilize risk/reward ratios to assess the expected returns of an investment relative to the level of risk they must assume to achieve those returns. A lower risk/return ratio is typically more favorable, as it indicates less risk for an equivalent potential gain.  Let's consider an example: an investment with a risk-reward ratio of 1:7 implies that an investor is willing to risk $1 for the opportunity to earn $7. In contrast, a risk/reward ratio of 1:3 suggests that an investor should expect to invest $1 in order to potentially earn $3 on their investment.
